   tatra bhagavān punarapi candraprabhaṃ kumārabhūtamāmantrayate sma  	tatra BagavAn punar api candra praBam kumAra BUtam Amantrayate sma  
   tasmāttarhi kumāra ya ākāṅkṣed bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ kimityahaṃ	tasmAt tarhi kumAra yaH AkAFkzet boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH kim iti aham
   sarvadharmāṇāṃ svabhāvaṃ kathaṃ jānīyāmiti,tena kumāra bodhisattvena	sarva DarmANAm svaBAvam kaTam jAnIyAm iti,tena kumAra boDisattvena
   mahāsattvena ayaṃ sarvadharmasvabhāvasamatāvipañcitaḥ samādhiḥ śrotavya	mahAsattvena ayam sarva Darma svaBAva samatA vipaQcitaH samADiH Srotavya
   udgrahītavyaḥ paryavāptavyo dhārayitavyo vācayitavya uddeṣṭavyaḥ	udgrahItavyaH paryavAptavyaH DArayitavyaH vAcayitavyaH uddezwavyaH
   svādhyātavyaḥ araṇābhāvanayā bhāvayitavyo bahulīkartavyaḥ parebhyaśca	svADyAtavyaH araNa aBAvanayA BAvayitavyaH bahulIkartavyaH pareByaH ca
   vistareṇa saṃprakāśayitavyaḥ ||	vistareNa saMprakASayitavyaH ||
   atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata  	aTa Kalu BagavAn= tasyAm velAyAm imAH gATAH aBAzata  
   tasyo rāgu na jātu kupyate na ca doṣo tasyo moha na jātu kupyate	tasyaH rAgu na jAtu kupyate na ca dozaH tasyaH moha na jAtu kupyate
   vṛṣabhisya /	vRzaBisya /
   teno sarvi kileśa cchoritānavaśeṣā yo 'sau dharmasvabhāvu jānatī	teno sarvi kila ISa cCorita an avaSezAH yaH asO Darma svaBAvu jAnatI
   supraśāntam // SRS_31.1 //	su praSAntam // SRs _31.1 //
   so 'sau śikṣa na jātu oṣirī sugatānāṃ so 'sau śūru na jātu istriyāṇāṃ	saH asO Sikza na jAtu ozirI sugatAnAm saH asO SUru na jAtu istriyANAm
   vaśameti /	vaSam eti /
   so 'sau śāsani prīti vindate sugatānāṃ yo 'sau dharmasvabhāvu jānatī	saH asO SAsani prIti vindate sugatAnAm yaH asO Darma svaBAvu jAnatI
   supraśāntam // SRS_31.2 //	su praSAntam // SRs _31.2 //
   so 'sau jñānavidhijña paṇḍito matimāṃśca so 'sau buddha ananta paśyatī	saH asO jQAna viDi jQa paNxitaH matimAn= ca saH asO budDa ananta paSyatI
   aparyantāṃ /	aparyantAm /
   so 'sau dhāraṇijñānu jānatī aparyantaṃ yo 'sau dharmasvabhāvu jānatī	saH asO DAraNi jQA anu jAnatI aparyantam yaH asO Darma svaBAvu jAnatI
   nayayuktim // SRS_31.3 //	naya yuktim // SRs _31.3 //
   so 'sau neha cireṇa bheṣyati dvipadendraḥ so 'sau vaidyu bhiṣaku bheṣyate	saH asO na iha cireNa Bezyati dvipada indraH saH asO vEdyu Bizaku Bezyate
   sukhadātā /	suKa dAtA /
   so 'sau uddhari śalya sarvaśo dukhitānāṃ yo 'sau dharmasvabhāvu jānatī	saH asO udDari Salya sarvaSas duKitAnAm yaH asO Darma svaBAvu jAnatI
   supraśāntam // SRS_31.4 //	su praSAntam // SRs _31.4 //
   so 'sau āturu jñātva duḥkhitānimi sattvān so 'sau bherī sadā parāhanī	saH asO Aturu jQAtva duHKitA nimi sattvAn saH asO BerI sadA parAhanI
   amṛtasya /	amRtasya /
   so 'sau bheṣyati nāyako jino nacireṇa yo 'sau dharmasvabhāvu jānatī	saH asO Bezyati nAyakaH jinaH nacireNa yaH asO Darma svaBAvu jAnatI
   supraśāntam // SRS_31.5 //	su praSAntam // SRs _31.5 //
   (Vaidya 191)	(VEdyaH 191)
   so 'sau bhaiṣajyanayeṣu kovido varavaidyo ādiṃ jānati sarvavyādhināṃ yatra	saH asO BEzajya nayezu kovidaH vara vEdyaH Adim jAnati sarva vyADinAm yatra

   // SRS_31.6 //	// SRs _31.6 //

   piṇḍam /	piNxam /
   so 'sau bodhivarāya sthāpayi bahusattvān yo 'sau dharmasvabhāvu jānatī	saH asO boDi varAya sTApayi bahu sattvAn yaH asO Darma svaBAvu jAnatI
   supraśāntam // SRS_31.7 //	su praSAntam // SRs _31.7 //
   so 'sau kṣāntibalena udgato naracandraḥ so 'sau loṣṭakadaṇḍatāḍito na ca	saH asO kzAnti balena udgataH nara candraH saH asO lozwaka daNxa tAxitaH na ca
   kupyī /	kupyI /
   so 'sau chidyatu aṅgamaṅgaśo na ca kṣubhye yo 'sau dharmasvabhāvu jānatī	saH asO Cidyatu aFgam aFgaSaH na ca kzuBye yaH asO Darma svaBAvu jAnatI
   supraśāntam // SRS_31.8 //	su praSAntam // SRs _31.8 //
   so 'sau kṣāntibale pratiṣṭhito balavanto so 'sau kṣāntiya vastu tādṛśo	saH asO kzAnti bale pratizWitaH balavantaH saH asO kzAntiya vastu tAdRSaH 
   supraśāntaḥ /	su praSAntaH /
   so 'sau kṣāntibalena manyate matiśūro yo 'sau dharmasvabhāvu jānatī	saH asO kzAnti balena manyate mati SUraH yaH asO Darma svaBAvu jAnatI
   supraśāntam // SRS_31.9 //	su praSAntam // SRs _31.9 //
   so 'sau vastu na jātu manyate ahu cchinnā teno sarvi bhavā vibhāvitāḥ sada	saH asO vastu na jAtu manyate ahu cCinnA teno sarvi BavAH viBAvitAH sada
   śūnyāḥ /	SUnyAH /
   tasyo saṃjñā prahīṇa sarvaśo nikhileno yo 'sau dharmasvabhāvu jānatī	tasyaH saMjQA prahINa sarvaSas niKilenaH yaH asO Darma svaBAvu jAnatI
   supraśāntam // SRS_31.10 //	su praSAntam // SRs _31.10 //
   te te dharmasvabhāvu deśayī supraṇītaṃ te te bodhi spṛśī anuttarāṃ	te te Darma svaBAvu deSayI su praNItam te te boDi spRSI anuttarAm
   nacireṇa /	nacireNa /
   yeṣāṃ dharmasvabhāvu gocaraḥ sunidhyapto teṣāṃ datta ananta dakṣiṇā	yezAm Darma svaBAvu gocaraH su niDi aptaH tezAm datta ananta dakziNA
   aparyantā // SRS_31.11 //	aparyantAH // SRs _31.11 //
   so 'sau bhāṣati sūtrakoṭiyo aparyantā yatha gaṅganadīya vālikāstatu bhūyaḥ	saH asO BAzati sUtra kowiyaH aparyantAH yaTa gaFga nadIya vAlikAH tatu BUyas 
   no cāsyu pratibhānu chidyate varṇamāne yo 'sau dharmasvabhāvu jānatī	no ca asyu pratiBA anu Cidyate varNamAne yaH asO Darma svaBAvu jAnatI
   supraśāntam // SRS_31.12 //	su praSAntam // SRs _31.12 //
   so 'sau kalpasahasrakoṭiśo nayutāni jñāneno sada bhoti udgato yatha meruḥ	saH asO kalpa sahasra kowiSas na yutAni jQAneno sada Boti udgataH yaTa meruH
   (Vaidya 192)	(VEdyaH 192)
   dharma tasya kṣayo na vidyate bhaṇamāne yo 'sau dharmasvabhāvu jānatī	Darma tasya kzayaH na vidyate BaNa mAne yaH asO Darma svaBAvu jAnatI
   supraśāntam // SRS_31.13 //	su praSAntam // SRs _31.13 //
   vistīrṇaṃ vipulaṃ acintiyaṃ pratibhānaṃ bhotī bodhivarāṃ gaveṣataḥ sada	vistIrNam vipulam acintiyam pratiBAnam BotI boDi varAm gavezataH sada
   tasyo /	tasyaH /

   supraśāntam // SRS_31.14 //	su praSAntam // SRs _31.14 //
   yaṃ caite dvipadottamā jinā bhaṇi dharmaṃ sarvaṃ taṃ ca śruṇitva gṛhṇatī	yam ca ete dvipada uttamA jinAH BaNi Darmam sarvam tam ca SruNi tva gRhNatI
   paripūrṇam /	paripUrNam /

   dharmān // SRS_31.15 //	DarmAn // SRH _31.15 //
   so 'sau bhoti viśiṣṭa tyāgavān sada kālaṃ bhotī dānapatiḥ sukhaṃdado	saH asO Boti viSizwa tyAgavAn sada kAlam BotI dAnapatiH suKaMdadaH 
   dukhitānām /	duKitAnAm /

   śūnyam // SRS_31.16 //	SUnyam // SRs _31.16 //
   sau 'sau jambudhvaje bhaviṣyatī sada rājā sattvānāṃ sada saukhya kāhitī	sO asO jambuDvaje BavizyatI sada rAjA sattvAnAm sada sOKya kAhitI
   aparyantam /	aparyantam /
   maitrāye samupetu prāṇīnāṃ sada kāle yo 'sau dharmasvabhāvu jānatī sada	mEtrAye samupetu prANInAm sada kAle yaH asO Darma svaBAvu jAnatI sada
   śūnyam // SRS_31.17 //	SUnyam // SRs _31.17 //

   rājyam /	rAjyam /

   śūnyam // SRS_31.18 //	SUnyam // SRs _31.18 //

   'pi /	api /
   teno pūjita bhonti nāyakā dvipadendrā yo 'sau dharmasvabhāvu jānatī sada	teno pUjita Bonti nAyakAH dvipada indrAH yaH asO Darma svaBAvu jAnatI sada
   śūnyam // SRS_31.19 //	SUnyam // SRs _31.19 //

   tehī satkṛta sarvi nāyakā sthita ye co yo 'sau dharmasvabhāvu jānatī sada	tehI satkRta sarvi nAyakA sTitaH ye caH yaH asO Darma svaBAvu jAnatI sada
   śūnyam // SRS_31.20 //	SUnyam // SRs _31.20 //
   (Vaidya 193)	(VEdyaH 193)
   so 'sau kośa dhareti paṇḍitaḥ sugatānāṃ so 'sau dhāraṇiye pratiṣṭhitaḥ	saH asO koSa DarA iti paNxitaH sugatAnAm saH asO DAraNiye pratizWitaH
   paramāyām /	paramAyAm /

   bahukalpān /	bahu kalpAn /

   // SRS_31.22 //	// SRs _31.22 //

   pacco tasya abhijña bhāvitā imi nityaṃ purataḥ so sugatāna sthāsyatī sada	pad caH tasya aBijQa BAvitAH imi nityam puratas saH sugatAna sTAsyatI sada
   śūraḥ // SRS_31.23 //	SUraH // SRs _31.23 //

   sattvāḥ // SRS_31.24 //	sattvAH // SRs _31.24 //

   // SRS_31.26 //	// SRs _31.26 //

   (Vaidya 194)	(VEdyaH 194)

   prapatanti // SRS_31.28 //	prapatanti // SRH _31.28 //

   32 Sūtradhāraṇānuśaṃsāparivartaḥ |	32 SUtra DAraNa anuSaMsA parivartaH |
   atha khalu bhagavān punareva candraprabhaṃ kumārabhūtamāmantrayate sma  	aTa Kalu BagavAn punar eva candra praBam kumAra BUtam Amantrayate sma  
   tasmāttarhi kumāra bodhisattvena mahāsattvena mahābhijñāparikarma	tasmAt tarhi kumAra boDisattvena mahAsattvena mahA aBijQA parikarma
   dhārayitukāmenāyaṃ samādhirdhārayitavyaḥ udgrahītavyaḥ paryavāptavyo	DArayitu kAmena ayam samADiH DArayitavyaH udgrahItavyaH paryavAptavyaH 
   dhārayitavyo vācayitavyaḥ pravartayitavyaḥ uddeṣṭavyaḥ svādhyātavyo	DArayitavyaH vAcayitavyaH pravartayitavyaH uddezwavyaH su ADyAtavyaH 
   bhāvayitavyaḥ, parebhyaśca vistareṇa saṃprakāśayitavya | katamacca tat	BAvayitavyaH, pareByaH ca vistareNa saMprakASayitavyaH | katamat ca tat 
   kumāra sarvadharmāṇāmabhijñāparikarma? yaduta sarvadharmāṇāmaparigrahaḥ	kumAra sarva DarmANAm aBijQA parikarma? yat uta sarva DarmANAm aparigrahaH
   aparāmarśaḥ śīlaskandhasyāmanyanā samādhiskandhasya apracāraḥ	aparAmarSaH SIla skanDasya amanyanA samADi skanDasya apracAraH
   prajñāskandhasya vivekadarśanaṃ vimuktiskandhasya yathābhūtadarśanaṃ	prajQA skanDasya viveka darSanam vimukti skanDasya yaTABUta darSanam
   vimuktijñānadarśanaskandhasya svabhāvaśūnyatādarśanaṃ sarvadharmāṇām |	vimukti jQAna darSana skanDasya svaBAva SUnyatA darSanam sarva DarmANAm |
   yayābhijñayā samanvāgato bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sarvasamādhivikurvitāni	yayA aBijQayA samanvAgataH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH sarva samADi vikurvitAni
   vikurvan sarvasattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśayati | idamucyate kumāra	vikurvan sarva sattvAnAm Darmam deSayati | idam ucyate kumAra
   mahābhijñāparikarmeti ||	mahA aBijQA parikarma iti ||
   atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata  	aTa Kalu BagavAn= tasyAm velAyAm imAH gATAH aBAzata  
   mahābhijñāparikarma avivādena deśitam /	mahA aBijQA parikarma avivAdena deSitam /
   vivāde yastu carati sodgṛhṇan na vimucyate // SRS_32.1 //	vivAde yaH tu carati sa udgRhNan na vimucyate // SRs _32.1 //
   abhijñā tasya sā prajñā bauddhaṃ jñānamacintiyam /	aBijQA tasya sA prajQA bOdDam jQAnam acintiyam /
   udgrahe yaḥ sthito bhoti jñānaṃ tasya na vidyate // SRS_32.2 //	udgrahe yaH sTitaH Boti jQAnam tasya na vidyate // SRs _32.2 //
   bahavo 'cintiyā dharmā ye śabdena prakāśitāḥ /	bahavaH acintiyAH DarmAH ye Sabdena prakASitAH /
   yastatra niviśecchabde saṃghābhāṣyaṃ na jānati // SRS_32.3 //	yaH tatra niviSet Sabde saMGABAzyam na jAnati // SRs _32.3 //
   saṃghābhāṣyamajānānaḥ kiṃ saṃghāya tu bhāṣitam /	saMGa ABAzyam aja AnAnaH kim saMGAya tu BAzitam /
   adharmaṃ bhāṣate dharmaṃ dharmatāyāmaśikṣitaḥ // SRS_32.4 //	aDarmam BAzate Darmam Darma tAyAm aSikzitaH // SRs _32.4 //
   lokadhātusahasreṣu ye mayā sūtra bhāṣitāḥ /	loka DAtu sahasrezu ye mayA sUtra BAzitAH /
   nānāvyañjana ekārthā na śakyaṃ parikīrtitum // SRS_32.5 //	nAnA vyaQjanaH eka arTAH na Sakyam parikIrtitum // SRs _32.5 //
   ekaṃ padārthaṃ cintetvā sarve te bhonti bhāvitāḥ /	ekam padArTam cintetvA sarve te Bonti BAvitAH /

   (Vaidya 303)	(VEdyaH 303)
   40 Parīndanāparivartaḥ |	40 ParIndanA parivartaH |
   atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata  	aTa Kalu BagavAn= tasyAm velAyAm imAH gATAH aBAzata  
   vipulā buddhadharmā hi vipulo deśito nayaḥ /	vipulA budDa DarmA hi vipulaH deSitaH nayaH /
   vipulaṃ dharma deśitvā vipulāṃllabhate guṇān // SRS_40.1 //	vipulam Darma deSitvA vipulAn= laBate guNAn // SRH _40.1 //
   yathā vipulamākāśamevaṃ dharmāṇa lakṣaṇam /	yaTA vipulam AkASam evam DarmANa lakzaNam /
   ratnāni vipulānyatra tasmādvaipulyamucyate // SRS_40.2 //	ratnAni vipulAni atra tasmAt vEpulyam ucyate // SRs _40.2 //
   vipulā cari sattvānāṃ vipulā teṣu deśitā /	vipulA cari sattvAnAm vipulA tezu deSitA /
   vipulo āgamo yasya tasmādvaipulyamucyate // SRS_40.3 //	vipulaH AgamaH yasya tasmAt vEpulyam ucyate // SRs _40.3 //
   asmin khalu punaḥ sarvadharmasvabhāvasamatāvipañcitasamādhinirdeśe	asmin Kalu punar sarva Darma svaBAva samatA vipaQcita sama aDi nirdeSe
   dharmaparyāye bhāṣyamāṇe aprameyaiḥ sattvairanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau	Darma paryAye BAzyamANe aprameyEH sattvEH anuttarAyAm samyaksaMboDO
   cittānyutpāditāni, aprameyāśca sattvā avaivartikā abhūvannanuttarāyāṃ	cittAni utpAditAni, aprameyAH ca sattvAH avEvartikA aBUvan= anuttarAyAm
   samyaksaṃbodhau | aprameyāṇāṃ ca sattvānāṃ pratyekabodhau ciattamutpannam	samyaksaMboDO | aprameyANAm ca sattvAnAm pratyeka boDO ciattam utpannam
   | aprameyāṇāṃ ca sattvānāmarhattvaphalasākṣātkriyāyāṃ cittānyutpannāni |	| aprameyANAm ca sattvAnAm arhat tva Pala sAkzAt kriyAyAm cittAni utpannAni |
   ayaṃ ca trisāhasramahāsāhasralokadhātuḥ ṣaḍavikāraṃ kampitaḥ prakampitaḥ	ayam ca tri sAhasra mahA sAhasra lokaDAtuH zaz avikAram kampitaH prakampitaH
   saṃprakampitaḥ | calitaḥ pracalitaḥ saṃpracalitaḥ | vedhitaḥ pravedhitaḥ |	saMprakampitaH | calitaH pracalitaH saMpracalitaH | veDitaH praveDitaH |
   saṃpravedhitaḥ | kṣumitaḥ prakṣubhitaḥ saṃprakṣubhitaḥ | raṇitaḥ	saMpraveDitaH | kzumitaH prakzuBitaH saMprakzuBitaH | raNitaH
   praraṇitaḥ saṃpraraṇitaḥ | garjitaḥ pragarjitaḥ saṃpragarjitaḥ | pūrvā	praraNitaH saMpraraNitaH | garjitaH pragarjitaH saMpragarjitaH | pUrvA
   digavanamati paścimā digunnamati | paścimā digavanamati pūrvā digunnamati|	digavanam ati paScimA diS unnamati | paScimA digavanam ati pUrvA diS unnamati|
   uttarā digunnamati dakṣiṇā digavanamati | uttarā digavanamati dakṣiṇā	uttarA diS unnamati dakziNA digavanam ati | uttarA digavanam ati dakziNA
   digunnamati | antādavanamati madhyādunnamati | madhyādavanamati	diS unnamati | antAt avanam ati maDyAt unnamati | maDyAt avanamati
   antādunnamati | aprameyasya cāvabhāsasya loke prādurbhāvo 'bhūt | mahacca	antAt unnamati | aprameyasya ca avaBAsasya loke prAdurBAvaH aBUt | mahat ca
   divyagandhavarṣamabhiprāvarṣat | devatāśca mahāntaṃ divyaṃ	divya ganDa varzam aBiprAvarzat | devatAH ca mahAntam divyam
   puṣpavarṣamutsṛjanti sma | divyāni ca tūryaśatasahasrāṇyuparyantarīkṣe	puzpa varzam utsRjanti sma | divyAni ca tUrya Sata sahasrANi upari antarIkze
   bhrāmayanti | evaṃ ca vācamabhāṣanta  	BrAmayanti | evam ca vAcam aBAzanta  
   sulabdhā lābhāsteṣāṃ sattvānāṃ ya imaṃ mahākaruṇāvatāradharmaparyāyaṃ	su labDAH lABAH tezAm sattvAnAm yaH imam mahA karuNa avatAra Darma paryAyam
   śroṣyanti | bahubuddhaparyupāsitāste sattvā bhaviṣyanti ya imaṃ	Srozyanti | bahu budDa paryupAsitAH te sattvAH Bavizyanti yaH imam
   sarvadharmasvabhāvasamatāvipañcitasamādhiṃ punaḥ punaḥ śroṣyanti, śrutvā	sarva Darma svaBAva samatA vipaQcita samADim punar punar Srozyanti, SrutvA
   ca likhiṣyanti udgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti araṇābhāvanayā	ca liKizyanti udgrahIzyanti DArayizyanti paryavApsyanti araNa aBAvanayA
   bhāvayiṣyanti, bahulīkariṣyanti, parebhyaśca vistareṇa saṃprakāśayiṣyanti	BAvayizyanti, bahulIkarizyanti, pareByaH ca vistareNa saMprakASayizyanti
   | sarvasatvānāṃ te dakṣiṇīyā bhaviṣyanti ||	| sarva satvAnAm te dakziNIyAH Bavizyanti ||
   atha khalu bhagavānāyuṣmantamānandamāmantrayate sma   udgṛhvīṣva	aTa Kalu BagavAn Ayuzmantam Anandam Amantrayate sma  udgRhvIzva
   tvamānanda imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ dhāraya vācaya paryavāpnuhi, pareṣāṃ ca	tvam AnandaH imam Darma paryAyam DAraya vAcaya paryavApnuhi, parezAm ca
   vistareṇa saṃprakāśaya | atha khalvāyuṣmānānado bhagavantametadavocat   ko	vistareNa saMprakASaya | aTa Kalu AyuzmAn AnadaH Bagavantam etat avocat  kaH 
   nāmāyaṃ bhagavan dharmaparyāyaḥ, kathaṃ caina dhārayāmi? bhagavānāha  	nAma ayam Bagavan Darma paryAyaH, kaTam ca ena DArayAmi? BagavAn Aha  
   mahākaruṇāvatāro nāmānanda idaṃ sūtraṃ dhāraya |	mahA karuNa avatAraH nAma AnandaH idam sUtram DAraya |
   sarvadharmasamatāvipañcito nāma samādhiriti dhāraya | ānanda āha  	sarva Darma samatA vipaQcitaH nAma samADiH iti DAraya | AnandaH Aha  
   udgṛhīto me bhagavannayaṃ dharmaparyāya iti ||	udgRhItaH me Bagavan= ayam Darma paryAyaH iti ||
   (Vaidya 304) idamavocad bhagavān | āttamanāścandraprabhaḥ kumārabhūta	(VEdyaH 304) idam avocat BagavAn | Atta manAH candrapraBaH kumAra BUta 
   āyuṣmāṃścānandaḥ tāścatasraḥ parṣado bhikṣubhikṣuṇyupāsakopāsikāḥ aneke ca	AyuzmAn= ca AnandaH tAH catasraH parzadaH Bikzu BikzuNI upAsa kopAsikAH aneke ca
   śuddhāvāsakāyikā devaputrāḥ sadevamānuṣāsuragandharvaśca loko bhagavato	SudDAvAsa kAyikAH deva putrAH sa deva mAnuza asura ganDarvaH ca lokaH BagavataH 
   bhāṣitamabhyanandanniti ||	BAzitam aByanandan= iti ||
   ityāryasarvadharmasvabhāvasamatāvipañcitāt samādheryathālabdhaṃ	iti Arya sarva Darma svaBAva samatA vipaQcitAt samADeH yaTAlabDam
   samādhirājaṃ nāma mahāyānasūtraṃ parivarto nāma catvāriṃśatitamaṃ samāptam	samADirAjam nAma mahAyAna sUtram parivartaH nAma catvAriMSatitamam samAptam
   ye dharmā hetuprabhavā hetusteṣāṃ tathāgato hyavadat |	ye DarmAH hetu praBavAH hetuH tezAm taTAgataH hi avadat |
   teṣāṃ ca yo nirodha evaṃ vādī mahāśramaṇaḥ ||	tezAm ca yaH niroDaH evam vAdI mahA ASramaNaH ||
